--------------------------------------------------------
--  DDL for View EDM_DOC_V
--------------------------------------------------------

  CREATE OR REPLACE FORCE EDITIONABLE VIEW "HDOEDIMS"."EDM_DOC_V" ("A", "B", "C", "D", "E", "F", "G", "H", "I", "J", "K", "L", "M", "N", "O") AS SELECT "A","B","C","D","E","F","G","H","I","J","K","L","M","N", "O"
FROM(
    SELECT
           decode(t.doc_type,'DOCTYPE0','도면','문서') AS A,
           t.doc_no AS B,
           t.doc_name AS C,
           t.rev_no AS D,
           TO_CHAR(t.update_date, 'YYYY-MM-DD')AS E,
           treepath as F,
           (select edm_tree.TNAME from edm_tree where tid =t.dockind_id)as G,
           t.COM_DOC_NO AS H,
           t.dir_path I,
           t.org_file J,
           t.f_size K,
           t.new_file L,
           t.doc_seq M,
           t.ext N,
           t.item O
    from ( SELECT --f.ext || d.lock_status AS ext,
                  d.doc_no,
                  d.doc_name,
                  d.dockind_id,
                  d.doc_seq,
                  d.doc_type,
                  d.update_date,
                  d.rev_no,
                  d.com_doc_no,
                  GETTREEPATH(d.tree_id)as treepath,
                --  (SELECT decode(COUNT(*),0,0,DOC_SEQ)  FROM EDM_DOC_EXTEND_COL WHERE DOC_SEQ = D.DOC_SEQ group by doc_seq) as hasextcol,
                -- (select cd.cvalue from edm_code cd where d.grade_id = cd.code_id and cd.c_category = 'GRADE') as grade_id_value,
                -- '0' as mr_count,
                  dr.dir_path, f.org_file, f.f_size, f.new_file, f.ext, i.item
             FROM   edm_doc d,(SELECT DOC_NO, NVL(TRUNC(MAX(REV_SREV) / 10000),0) REV_NO, NVL(MOD(MAX(REV_SREV), 10000),0) SYS_REV_NO
                                 FROM (select *
                                                from EDM_DOC rev_doc,(SELECT auth_id
                                                                        FROM edm_role_mapping
                                                                       WHERE role_id =
                                                                             (SELECT role_id
                                                                                FROM edm_emp_role
                                                                               WHERE emp_id =  'admin' /**P*/
                                                                                 AND r_category = 'TREE')) rev_auth
                                               WHERE  tree_id In (  SELECT tid
                                                                      From edm_tree
                                                                START WITH tid =  'CI' /** 필수 분류코드*/
                                                          CONNECT BY PRIOR tid = pid)
                                                 and STATUS = 'E'--사용중인 도면만 조회
                                                 and rev_doc.tree_id = rev_auth.auth_id
                                              )
                                      GROUP BY DOC_NO) REV,
                           edm_file f,
					       edm_directory dr,
					       edm_item i
                    WHERE  d.tree_id IN (SELECT  auth_id
                                           FROM  edm_role_mapping
                                          WHERE  role_id =(SELECT  role_id
                                                             FROM  edm_emp_role
                                                            WHERE  emp_id =  'admin' /**필수  사용자 ID*/
                                                              AND  r_category = 'TREE')
                                        )
                      AND d.doc_no = rev.doc_no
                      AND d.sys_rev_no = rev.sys_rev_no(+)
                      AND d.rev_no = rev.rev_no(+)
                      And f.file_id = d.file_id
                      And f.dir_id  = dr.dir_id
                      AND STATUS = 'E'--사용중인 도면만 조회
				      AND d.doc_seq = i.doc_seq(+)
                      and d.tree_id In (  SELECT tid
                                            From edm_tree
                                      START WITH tid =  'CI' /** 필수 분류코드*/
                                     CONNECT BY PRIOR tid = pid)

                  ) t
)
/*   조회조건 */
WHERE 1=1
;
--------------------------------------------------------
--  DDL for View EDM_EMP_V
--------------------------------------------------------

  CREATE OR REPLACE FORCE EDITIONABLE VIEW "HDOEDIMS"."EDM_EMP_V" ("COMPANY_CODE", "COMPANY_NAME", "EMP_ID", "ORG_ID", "ORG_NAME", "DUTY_ID", "DUTY_NAME", "EMP_NAME", "EMP_PW", "EMP_EMAIL", "AUTH_START_DATE", "AUTH_END_DATE", "HOME_SVR_ID", "LANG_CODE", "EMP_NUM", "SVR_ID", "REGION_CODE", "REGION_NAME", "USE_YN") AS SELECT EDM_EMP.COMPANY_CODE,
        EDM_COMPANY.COMPANY_NAME,
        EDM_EMP.EMP_ID,
        EDM_EMP.ORG_ID,
        EDM_ORG.ORG_NAME,
        EDM_EMP.DUTY_ID,
        EDM_DUTY.DUTY_NAME,
        EDM_EMP.EMP_NAME,
        EDM_EMP.EMP_PW,
        EDM_EMP.EMP_EMAIL,
        EDM_EMP.AUTH_START_DATE,
        EDM_EMP.AUTH_END_DATE,
        EDM_EMP.HOME_SVR_ID,
        EDM_EMP.LANG_CODE,
        EDM_EMP.EMP_NUM,
        EDM_COMPANY.SVR_ID,
        EDM_EMP.REGION_CODE,
        EDM_EMP.REGION_NAME,
        EDM_EMP.USE_YN
   FROM EDM_EMP,
        EDM_ORG,
        EDM_DUTY,
        EDM_COMPANY
  WHERE EDM_EMP.ORG_ID = EDM_ORG.ORG_ID
    AND EDM_EMP.DUTY_ID = EDM_DUTY.DUTY_ID
    AND EDM_EMP.COMPANY_CODE = EDM_ORG.COMPANY_CODE
    AND EDM_EMP.COMPANY_CODE = EDM_COMPANY.COMPANY_CODE
    AND EDM_ORG.USE_YN = 'Y'
    AND EDM_DUTY.USE_YN = 'Y'
;

--  DDL for View EDM_OUT_COMPANY_V
--------------------------------------------------------

  CREATE OR REPLACE FORCE EDITIONABLE VIEW "HDOEDIMS"."EDM_OUT_COMPANY_V" ("COMPANY_CODE", "COMPANY_NAME", "COMPANY_KIND", "SVR_ID", "USE_YN", "CREATE_DATE", "CREATED_BY", "UPDATE_DATE", "UPDATED_BY") AS SELECT "COMPANY_CODE", "COMPANY_NAME", "COMPANY_KIND", "SVR_ID", "USE_YN", "CREATE_DATE", "CREATED_BY", "UPDATE_DATE", "UPDATED_BY" FROM EDM_COMPANY
WHERE COMPANY_KIND = 'O'
;
--------------------------------------------------------
--  DDL for View EDM_OUT_EMP_V
--------------------------------------------------------

  CREATE OR REPLACE FORCE EDITIONABLE VIEW "HDOEDIMS"."EDM_OUT_EMP_V" ("COMPANY_CODE", "EMP_ID", "EMP_NAME", "EMP_PW", "EMP_NUM", "ORG_ID", "DUTY_NAME", "EMP_EMAIL", "USE_YN", "CREATE_DATE", "UPDATE_DATE") AS SELECT EMP.COMPANY_CODE, 
                 EMP.EMP_ID, 
                 EMP.EMP_NAME, 
                 EMP.EMP_PW,
                 EMP.EMP_NUM, 
                 EMP.ORG_ID, 
                 DUTY.DUTY_NAME, 
                 EMP.EMP_EMAIL, 
                 EMP.USE_YN, 
                 EMP.CREATE_DATE, 
                 EMP.UPDATE_DATE
FROM  EDM_COMPANY  COMPANY INNER JOIN
            EDM_EMP  EMP ON COMPANY.COMPANY_CODE = EMP.COMPANY_CODE INNER JOIN
            EDM_DUTY  DUTY ON EMP.DUTY_ID = DUTY.DUTY_ID
WHERE (COMPANY.COMPANY_KIND = 'O')
;
--------------------------------------------------------
--  DDL for View EDM_OUT_ORG_V
--------------------------------------------------------

  CREATE OR REPLACE FORCE EDITIONABLE VIEW "HDOEDIMS"."EDM_OUT_ORG_V" ("COMPANY_CODE", "ORG_ID", "ORG_NAME", "PARENT_ID", "USE_YN", "CREATE_DATE", "UPDATE_DATE") AS SELECT ORG.COMPANY_CODE, ORG.ORG_ID, ORG.ORG_NAME, ORG.PARENT_ID,
ORG.USE_YN, ORG.CREATE_DATE, ORG.UPDATE_DATE FROM EDM_COMPANY COMPANY, EDM_ORG ORG
WHERE COMPANY_KIND = 'O'
AND COMPANY.COMPANY_CODE = ORG.COMPANY_CODE
;

,		PM_USER_ID
,		PM_USER_NAME
,		FULL_PATH
    FROM edm_tree a

--------------------------------------------------------
--  DDL for View MR_PM_EMP_V
--------------------------------------------------------

  CREATE OR REPLACE FORCE EDITIONABLE VIEW "HDOEDIMS"."MR_PM_EMP_V" ("CAPEX_NO", "MR_NO", "MR_REQ_TITLE", "EMP_ID", "EMP_NAME", "EMP_EMAIL") AS SELECT DISTINCT MST.CAPEX_NO, MST.MR_NO, MST.MR_REQ_TITLE, EMP.EMP_ID, EMP.EMP_NAME, EMP.EMP_EMAIL
FROM   MR_REQ_MST MST, MR_REQ_CHRGR_CHG_HIST MCH, EDM_EMP EMP
WHERE  MST.CAPEX_NO    IS NOT NULL
AND    MST.DEL_YN      = '0'
AND    MCH.DEL_YN      = '0'
AND    MST.MR_REQ_NO   = MCH.MR_REQ_NO
AND    MCH.CHRGR_CL_CD = 'Z02I'
AND    MCH.EFF_END_DTM = '99991231235959'
AND    MCH.CHRG_EMP_NO = EMP.EMP_ID
;
--------------------------------------------------------
--  DDL for View MR_REQ_MST_V
--------------------------------------------------------

  CREATE OR REPLACE FORCE EDITIONABLE VIEW "HDOEDIMS"."MR_REQ_MST_V" ("CAPEX_NO", "MR_REQ_NO", "MR_NO", "MR_REQ_TITLE", "EMPID_A", "NAME_A", "DEPTNM_A", "MAIL_A", "EMPID_D", "NAME_D", "DEPTNM_D", "MAIL_D", "EMPID_I", "NAME_I", "DEPTNM_I", "MAIL_I") AS SELECT DISTINCT MST.CAPEX_NO, MST.MR_REQ_NO, MST.MR_NO, MST.MR_REQ_TITLE
      , MCH1.EMP_ID AS EMPID_A, MCH1.EMP_NAME AS NAME_A, MCH1.THDAY_TEAM AS DEPTNM_A, MCH1.EMP_EMAIL AS MAIL_A
      , MCH2.EMP_ID AS EMPID_D, MCH2.EMP_NAME AS NAME_D, MCH2.THDAY_TEAM AS DEPTNM_D, MCH2.EMP_EMAIL AS MAIL_D
      , MCH3.EMP_ID AS EMPID_I, MCH3.EMP_NAME AS NAME_I, MCH3.THDAY_TEAM AS DEPTNM_I, MCH3.EMP_EMAIL AS MAIL_I
FROM   MR_REQ_MST MST
     ,(SELECT MH1.MR_REQ_NO, MH1.CHRG_EMP_NO, MH1.CHRG_TEAM_NO, EMP1.EMP_ID, EMP1.EMP_NAME, MH1.THDAY_TEAM, EMP1.EMP_EMAIL
       FROM   MR_REQ_CHRGR_CHG_HIST MH1
            , EDM_EMP EMP1
       WHERE  MH1.MR_REQ_PROC_STEP_DET_NO
            = (SELECT MAX(MR_REQ_PROC_STEP_DET_NO) DETNO
               FROM   MR_REQ_CHRGR_CHG_HIST MCH
               WHERE  MCH.CHRGR_CL_CD = 'Z02A'
               AND    MCH.EFF_END_DTM = '99991231235959'
               AND    MCH.THDAY_TEAM  IS NOT NULL
               AND    MCH.DEL_YN      = '0'
               AND    MH1.MR_REQ_NO   = MCH.MR_REQ_NO)
          AND  MH1.CHRG_EMP_NO  = EMP1.EMP_ID(+)) MCH1
     ,(SELECT MH2.MR_REQ_NO, MH2.CHRG_EMP_NO, MH2.CHRG_TEAM_NO, EMP2.EMP_ID, EMP2.EMP_NAME, MH2.THDAY_TEAM, EMP2.EMP_EMAIL
       FROM   MR_REQ_CHRGR_CHG_HIST MH2
            , EDM_EMP EMP2
       WHERE  MH2.MR_REQ_PROC_STEP_DET_NO
            = (SELECT MAX(MR_REQ_PROC_STEP_DET_NO) DETNO
               FROM   MR_REQ_CHRGR_CHG_HIST MCH
               WHERE  MCH.CHRGR_CL_CD = 'Z02D'
               AND    MCH.EFF_END_DTM = '99991231235959'
               AND    MCH.THDAY_TEAM  IS NOT NULL
               AND    MCH.DEL_YN      = '0'
               AND    MCH.MR_REQ_NO   = MH2.MR_REQ_NO)
          AND  MH2.CHRG_EMP_NO  = EMP2.EMP_ID(+)) MCH2
     ,(SELECT MH3.MR_REQ_NO, MH3.CHRG_EMP_NO, MH3.CHRG_TEAM_NO, EMP3.EMP_ID, EMP3.EMP_NAME, MH3.THDAY_TEAM, EMP3.EMP_EMAIL
       FROM   MR_REQ_CHRGR_CHG_HIST MH3
            , EDM_EMP EMP3
       WHERE  MH3.MR_REQ_PROC_STEP_DET_NO
            = (SELECT MAX(MR_REQ_PROC_STEP_DET_NO) DETNO
               FROM   MR_REQ_CHRGR_CHG_HIST MCH
               WHERE  MCH.CHRGR_CL_CD = 'Z02I'
               AND    MCH.EFF_END_DTM = '99991231235959'
               AND    MCH.THDAY_TEAM  IS NOT NULL
               AND    MCH.DEL_YN      = '0'
               AND    MH3.MR_REQ_NO   = MCH.MR_REQ_NO)
         AND  MH3.CHRG_EMP_NO  = EMP3.EMP_ID(+)) MCH3
WHERE  1 = 1
AND    MST.CAPEX_NO   IS NOT NULL
AND    MST.DEL_YN     =  '0'
AND    MST.PROC_ST_CD <> 'Z0143'
AND    MST.MR_REQ_NO  = MCH1.MR_REQ_NO(+)
AND    MST.MR_REQ_NO  = MCH2.MR_REQ_NO(+)
AND    MST.MR_REQ_NO  = MCH3.MR_REQ_NO(+)
ORDER BY 1
;
--------------------------------------------------------
--  DDL for View V_CHECK_WORK_RESULT
--------------------------------------------------------

  CREATE OR REPLACE FORCE EDITIONABLE VIEW "HDOEDIMS"."V_CHECK_WORK_RESULT" ("PLANT_NO", "PLANT_NAME", "DEPT_NO", "DEPT_NAME", "EQUIP_CODE", "CHECK_EQUIP_DESC", "RTDB_TAG", "CHECK_POINT_ITEM_NAME", "INPUT_DATE", "V_DATA", "UNIT", "NORMAL_UNDER", "NORMAL_UPPER", "CAUTION_UNDER", "CAUTION_UPPER", "CRITICAL_UNDER", "CRITICAL_UPPER") AS select PLANT_NO,PLANT_NAME,DEPT_NO,DEPT_NAME,EQUIP_CODE,CHECK_EQUIP_DESC,RTDB_TAG,CHECK_POINT_ITEM_NAME,INPUT_DATE,V_DATA,UNIT,NORMAL_UNDER,NORMAL_UPPER,CAUTION_UNDER,CAUTION_UPPER,CRITICAL_UNDER,CRITICAL_UPPER
from check_work_result
;
--------------------------------------------------------
--  DDL for View V_MR_PROCESS_DATA
--------------------------------------------------------

  CREATE OR REPLACE FORCE EDITIONABLE VIEW "HDOEDIMS"."V_MR_PROCESS_DATA" ("MR_REQ_NO", "MR_NO", "MR_REQ_TITLE", "PLANT", "MR_PROC_NO", "MR_EQUIP_CD", "LAST_CHG_DT_Z02A", "CHRG_EMP_NO_Z02A", "CHRG_TEAM_NO_Z02A", "THDAY_TEAM_Z02A", "CHRG_EMP_NO_Z02C1", "CHRG_EMP_NO_Z02C2", "CHRG_EMP_NO_Z02C3", "LAST_CHG_DT_Z02C1", "LAST_CHG_DT_Z02C2", "LAST_CHG_DT_Z02C3", "CHRG_EMP_NO_Z02D", "CHRG_EMP_NO_Z02I", "CHRG_EMP_NO_Z02G", "CHRG_EMP_NO_Z02G1", "REQ_CLCD", "REQ_CL_DTLCD", "WORK_PSBL_CLCD", "WORK_PSBL_CL_RSN", "CHRG_EMP_NO_Z02E", "RECOVERY_DT_Z02E", "ISSUE_CTT", "DRAW_MNG_NO_FILE_NM", "LAST_CHG_DT_Z0025", "LAST_CHG_DT_Z0030", "LAST_CHG_DT_Z0040", "LAST_CHG_DT_Z0050", "LAST_CHG_DT_Z0060", "LAST_CHG_DT_Z0070", "LAST_CHG_DT_Z0080", "LAST_CHG_DT_Z0090", "HAZOP_ACT_YN", "PORC_ACT_YN", "CHRG_EMP_NO_Z00R0", "LAST_CHG_DT_Z00R0", "CL_CTX_01", "CL_CTT_01", "CL_CTX_02", "CL_CTT_02", "CL_CTX_03", "CL_CTT_03", "CL_CTX_04", "CL_CTT_04", "CL_CTX_05", "CL_CTT_05", "CL_CTX_06", "CL_CTT_06", "CL_CTX_07", "CL_CTT_07", "CL_CTX_08", "CL_CTT_08", "MR_STEP_CD", "PROC_ST_CD", "FST_RGST_DT", "LAST_CHG_DT") AS SELECT DISTINCT
       M.MR_REQ_NO                            -- MR코드
     , M.MR_NO                                -- MR번호
     , M.MR_REQ_TITLE                         -- 사업명
     , M.PLANT                                -- 회사
     , UNIT.MR_PROC_NO                        -- 세부공정
     , EQUIP.MR_EQUIP_CD                      -- 관련설비
     , Z02A.LAST_CHG_DT  AS LAST_CHG_DT_Z02A     -- MR요청일자
     , Z02A.CHRG_EMP_NO  AS CHRG_EMP_NO_Z02A     -- MR요청자
     , Z02A.CHRG_TEAM_NO AS CHRG_TEAM_NO_Z02A    -- 요청부서코두
     , Z02A.THDAY_TEAM   AS THDAY_TEAM_Z02A      -- 요청부서명
     , Z02C1.CHRG_EMP_NO AS CHRG_EMP_NO_Z02C1    -- MR요청 1차 승인자
     , Z02C2.CHRG_EMP_NO AS CHRG_EMP_NO_Z02C2    -- MR요청 2차 승인자
     , Z02C3.CHRG_EMP_NO AS CHRG_EMP_NO_Z02C3    -- MR요청 3차 승인자
     , Z02C1.LAST_CHG_DT AS LAST_CHG_DT_Z02C1    -- MR요청 1차 승인일자
     , Z02C2.LAST_CHG_DT AS LAST_CHG_DT_Z02C2    -- MR요청 2차 승인일자
     , Z02C3.LAST_CHG_DT AS LAST_CHG_DT_Z02C3    -- MR요청 3차 승인일자
     , Z02D.CHRG_EMP_NO  AS CHRG_EMP_NO_Z02D     -- 기술검토 담당자
     , Z02I.CHRG_EMP_NO  AS CHRG_EMP_NO_Z02I     -- MR Project Engineer
     , Z02G.CHRG_EMP_NO  AS CHRG_EMP_NO_Z02G     -- 수행 팀장
     , Z02G1.CHRG_EMP_NO AS CHRG_EMP_NO_Z02G1    -- 수행팀 직책과장
     , (SELECT C.MR_COMM_NM FROM MR_COMM_COD C WHERE C.MR_COMM_GRP_CD = 'REQ' AND MR_COMM_CD = REQ_CL_CD) AS REQ_CLCD         -- 요청구분
     , (SELECT C.MR_COMM_NM FROM MR_COMM_COD C WHERE C.MR_COMM_GRP_CD = 'REQ_DET' AND MR_COMM_CD = REQ_CL_DTL_CD) AS REQ_CL_DTLCD   -- 요청구분상세
     , (SELECT C.MR_COMM_NM FROM MR_COMM_COD C WHERE C.MR_COMM_GRP_CD = 'WORK' AND MR_COMM_CD = WORK_PSBL_CL_CD) AS WORK_PSBL_CLCD  -- 작업시점
     , M.WORK_PSBL_CL_RSN                     -- 작업시점 기간
     , Z02E.CHRG_EMP_NO      AS CHRG_EMP_NO_Z02E -- 원상복구책임자
     , Z02E.FST_PROC_TRM_DT  AS RECOVERY_DT_Z02E -- 원상복구기한
     , M.ISSUE_CTT                             -- 문제내용
     , ATTACH.DRAW_MNG_NO_FILE_NM AS DRAW_MNG_NO_FILE_NM       -- 도면번호 , 첨부파일명
     , Z0025.LAST_CHG_DT  AS LAST_CHG_DT_Z0025 -- 직무검토(1) 일자
     , Z0030.LAST_CHG_DT  AS LAST_CHG_DT_Z0030 -- 타당성검토 일자
     , Z0040.LAST_CHG_DT  AS LAST_CHG_DT_Z0040 -- 직무검토(2) 일자
     , Z0050.LAST_CHG_DT  AS LAST_CHG_DT_Z0050 -- 투자지출품의 일자
     , Z0060.LAST_CHG_DT  AS LAST_CHG_DT_Z0060 -- MR수행 완료 일자
     , Z0070.LAST_CHG_DT  AS LAST_CHG_DT_Z0070 -- 가동전안전점검 일자
     , Z0080.LAST_CHG_DT  AS LAST_CHG_DT_Z0080 -- 자교등록 일자
     , Z0090.LAST_CHG_DT  AS LAST_CHG_DT_Z0090 -- MR완료 일자
     , M.HAZOP_ACT_YN                          -- HAZOP 대상여부
     , M.PORC_ACT_YN                           -- PORC 여부(Y:필요, S:공유, N:불필요)
     , Z00R0.CHRG_EMP_NO  AS CHRG_EMP_NO_Z00R0 -- 위험성검토자
     , Z00R0.LAST_CHG_DT  AS LAST_CHG_DT_Z00R0 -- 위험성검토일자
     , '설비 변경에 따른 기존 설계 운전(유량/온도/압력) 조건 초과 시
(단, 유량의 경우 Design조건의 10% 이하는 미실시함)' AS CL_CTX_01 -- 1번 내용
     , Z00RC.CL_CTT_01                        -- 1번 값
     , '공정 원료 변경 사항이 있을 시' AS  CL_CTX_02    -- 2번 내용
     , Z00RC.CL_CTT_02                        -- 2번 값
     , 'Control logic / Interlock logic 등의 변경 사항이 있을 시
(단,  Control logic 의 경우는 설비 변경 시에만 적용함)' AS  CL_CTX_03   -- 3번내용
     , Z00RC.CL_CTT_03                        -- 3번 값
     , 'Control valve 설치 시'  AS CL_CTX_04     -- 4번 내용
     , Z00RC.CL_CTT_04                        -- 4번 값
     , 'Relief load에 따른 변경 사항이 있을 시' AS CL_CTX_05    -- 5번 내용
     , Z00RC.CL_CTT_05                        -- 5번 값
     , ' ' AS CL_CTX_06                       -- 6번 내용
     , Z00RC.CL_CTT_06                        -- 6번 값
     , '공정 또는 설비의 용도 변경이 있을 시' AS CL_CTX_07 -- 7번 내용
     , Z00RC.CL_CTT_07                        -- 7번 값
     , '이외 해당 기술팀 팀장이 설비 변경에 따른 신규 공정 위험성 평가가 필요하다고 판단될 경우' AS CL_CTX_08 -- 8번 내용
     , Z00RC.CL_CTT_08                        -- 8번 값
     --, TRV.FST_RGST_DT AS FST_RGST_DT_Z02D
     , M.MR_STEP_CD
     , M.PROC_ST_CD
     , M.FST_RGST_DT
     , M.LAST_CHG_DT
FROM   MR_REQ_MST M,        -- MR 마스터
      (SELECT *
         FROM MR_REQ_CHRGR_CHG_HIST H
        WHERE EXISTS (SELECT *
                        FROM MR_REQ_PROC_STEP S
                            ,MR_REQ_PROC_STEP_DET D
                       WHERE S.MR_REQ_PROC_STEP_NO = D.MR_REQ_PROC_STEP_NO
                         AND S.MR_STEP_CD = 'Z0010'
                         AND S.DEL_YN = '0'
                         AND D.DEL_YN = '0'
                         AND D.PROC_ST_CD  = 'Z0121'
                         AND D.MR_REQ_PROC_STEP_DET_NO = H.MR_REQ_PROC_STEP_DET_NO)
          AND H.EFF_END_DTM = '99991231235959'
          AND H.CHRGR_CL_CD = 'Z02A'
          AND H.DEL_YN = '0'
          AND H.PROC_ST_CD IN ('Z0110','Z0141')) Z02A,  -- MR요청자
      (SELECT *
         FROM MR_REQ_CHRGR_CHG_HIST H
        WHERE EXISTS (SELECT *
                        FROM MR_REQ_PROC_STEP S
                            ,MR_REQ_PROC_STEP_DET D
                       WHERE S.MR_REQ_PROC_STEP_NO = D.MR_REQ_PROC_STEP_NO
                         AND S.MR_STEP_CD = 'Z0010'
                         AND S.DEL_YN = '0'
                         AND D.DEL_YN = '0'
                         AND D.PROC_ST_CD  = 'Z0121'
                         AND D.MR_REQ_PROC_STEP_DET_NO = H.MR_REQ_PROC_STEP_DET_NO)
          AND H.EFF_END_DTM = '99991231235959'
          AND H.CHRGR_CL_CD = 'Z02C'
          AND H.DEL_YN      = '0'
          AND H.PROC_ST_CD  = 'Z0121') Z02C1,  -- MR요청 1차 승인자
      (SELECT *
         FROM MR_REQ_CHRGR_CHG_HIST H
        WHERE EXISTS (SELECT *
                        FROM MR_REQ_PROC_STEP S
                            ,MR_REQ_PROC_STEP_DET D
                       WHERE S.MR_REQ_PROC_STEP_NO = D.MR_REQ_PROC_STEP_NO
                         AND S.MR_STEP_CD = 'Z0010'
                         AND S.DEL_YN = '0'
                         AND D.DEL_YN = '0'
                         AND D.PROC_ST_CD  = 'Z0122'
                         AND D.MR_REQ_PROC_STEP_DET_NO = H.MR_REQ_PROC_STEP_DET_NO)
          AND H.EFF_END_DTM = '99991231235959'
          AND H.CHRGR_CL_CD = 'Z02C'
          AND H.DEL_YN      = '0'
          AND H.PROC_ST_CD  = 'Z0121') Z02C2,  -- MR요청 1차 승인자
      (SELECT *
         FROM MR_REQ_CHRGR_CHG_HIST H
        WHERE EXISTS (SELECT *
                        FROM MR_REQ_PROC_STEP S
                            ,MR_REQ_PROC_STEP_DET D
                       WHERE S.MR_REQ_PROC_STEP_NO = D.MR_REQ_PROC_STEP_NO
                         AND S.MR_STEP_CD = 'Z0010'
                         AND S.DEL_YN = '0'
                         AND D.DEL_YN = '0'
                         AND D.PROC_ST_CD  = 'Z0132'
                         AND D.MR_REQ_PROC_STEP_DET_NO = H.MR_REQ_PROC_STEP_DET_NO)
          AND H.EFF_END_DTM = '99991231235959'
          AND H.CHRGR_CL_CD = 'Z02C'
          AND H.DEL_YN      = '0'
          AND H.PROC_ST_CD  = 'Z0122') Z02C3,  -- MR요청 2차 승인자    ,  -- MR요청 1차 승인자
      (SELECT *
         FROM MR_REQ_CHRGR_CHG_HIST H
        WHERE EXISTS (SELECT *
                        FROM MR_REQ_PROC_STEP S
                            ,MR_REQ_PROC_STEP_DET D
                       WHERE S.MR_REQ_PROC_STEP_NO = D.MR_REQ_PROC_STEP_NO
                         AND S.MR_STEP_CD = 'Z0020'
                         AND S.DEL_YN = '0'
                         AND D.DEL_YN = '0'
                         AND D.PROC_ST_CD  = 'Z0121'
                         AND D.MR_REQ_PROC_STEP_DET_NO = H.MR_REQ_PROC_STEP_DET_NO)
          AND H.EFF_END_DTM = '99991231235959'
          AND H.CHRGR_CL_CD = 'Z02D'
          AND H.DEL_YN      = '0'
          AND H.PROC_ST_CD  = 'Z0110') Z02D,  -- MR 기술검토자
      (SELECT *
         FROM MR_REQ_CHRGR_CHG_HIST H
        WHERE EXISTS (SELECT *
                        FROM MR_REQ_PROC_STEP S
                            ,MR_REQ_PROC_STEP_DET D
                       WHERE S.MR_REQ_PROC_STEP_NO = D.MR_REQ_PROC_STEP_NO
                         AND S.MR_STEP_CD = 'Z0030'
                         AND S.DEL_YN = '0'
                         AND D.DEL_YN = '0'
--                         AND D.PROC_ST_CD  = 'Z0133'
                         AND D.MR_REQ_PROC_STEP_DET_NO = H.MR_REQ_PROC_STEP_DET_NO)
          AND H.EFF_END_DTM = '99991231235959'
          AND H.CHRGR_CL_CD = 'Z02I'
          AND H.DEL_YN      = '0') Z02I,  -- MR Project Engineer
      (SELECT *
         FROM MR_REQ_CHRGR_CHG_HIST H
        WHERE EXISTS (SELECT *
                        FROM MR_REQ_PROC_STEP S
                            ,MR_REQ_PROC_STEP_DET D
                       WHERE S.MR_REQ_PROC_STEP_NO = D.MR_REQ_PROC_STEP_NO
                         AND S.MR_STEP_CD = 'Z0030'
                         AND S.DEL_YN = '0'
--                         AND D.DEL_YN = '0'
                         AND D.PROC_ST_CD IN ( 'Z0110' , 'Z0121')
                         AND D.MR_REQ_PROC_STEP_DET_NO = H.MR_REQ_PROC_STEP_DET_NO)
          AND H.EFF_END_DTM = '99991231235959'
          AND H.CHRGR_CL_CD = 'Z02G'
          AND H.DEL_YN      = '0') Z02G,  -- MR수행 팀장
      (SELECT MR_REQ_NO, listagg(CHRG_EMP_NO,',') WITHIN GROUP(ORDER BY CHRG_EMP_NO) AS CHRG_EMP_NO
         FROM MR_REQ_CHRGR_CHG_HIST H
        WHERE EXISTS (SELECT *
                        FROM MR_REQ_PROC_STEP S
                            ,MR_REQ_PROC_STEP_DET D
                       WHERE S.MR_REQ_PROC_STEP_NO = D.MR_REQ_PROC_STEP_NO
                         AND S.MR_STEP_CD = 'Z0030'
                         AND S.DEL_YN = '0'
--                         AND D.DEL_YN = '0'
                         AND D.PROC_ST_CD  IN ('Z0110', 'Z0121')
                         AND D.MR_REQ_PROC_STEP_DET_NO = H.MR_REQ_PROC_STEP_DET_NO)
          AND H.EFF_END_DTM = '99991231235959'
          AND H.CHRGR_CL_CD = 'Z02G1'
          AND H.DEL_YN      = '0'
          AND H.PROC_ST_CD  IN ('Z0110', 'Z0121')
        GROUP BY H.MR_REQ_NO) Z02G1,   -- MR수행직책과장
      (SELECT P.MR_REQ_NO, L.WERKS, listagg(P.MR_PROC_NO || ' ' || L.KTEXT,',') WITHIN GROUP(ORDER BY P.MR_PROC_NO || ' ' || L.KTEXT) AS MR_PROC_NO
         FROM MR_REQ_PROC P, SAP_LOCA L
        WHERE P.DEL_YN = '0'
          AND P.MR_PROC_NO = L.STAND
        GROUP BY P.MR_REQ_NO, L.WERKS) UNIT,  -- 세부공정
      (SELECT ME.MR_REQ_NO, listagg(ME.MR_EQUIP_CD || ' ' || SE.EQKTX,',') WITHIN GROUP(ORDER BY ME.MR_EQUIP_CD || ' ' || SE.EQKTX) AS MR_EQUIP_CD
         FROM (SELECT MR_REQ_NO, MR_EQUIP_CD
                 FROM (SELECT MR_REQ_NO, MR_EQUIP_CD,
                              ROW_NUMBER() OVER (PARTITION BY MR_REQ_NO ORDER BY MR_REQ_NO DESC) AS ROW_NUM
                         FROM MR_REQ_EQUIP
                        WHERE DEL_YN = '0') T1
                WHERE ROW_NUM <= 15) ME
            , SAP_EQUIP SE
        WHERE ME.MR_EQUIP_CD  = SE.EQUNR
        GROUP BY ME.MR_REQ_NO) EQUIP,    -- 관련설비                                                                                          -- 3270
      (SELECT H.MR_REQ_NO, H.CHRG_EMP_NO, T1.FST_PROC_TRM_DT
         FROM MR_REQ_CHRGR_CHG_HIST H
            ,(SELECT *
                FROM MR_REQ_PROC_STEP S
                    ,MR_REQ_PROC_STEP_DET D
               WHERE S.MR_REQ_PROC_STEP_NO = D.MR_REQ_PROC_STEP_NO
                 AND S.MR_STEP_CD = 'Z0010'
                 AND S.DEL_YN = '0'
                 AND D.DEL_YN = '0'
                 AND D.PROC_ST_CD  = 'Z0110') T1
        WHERE T1.MR_REQ_PROC_STEP_DET_NO = H.MR_REQ_PROC_STEP_DET_NO
          AND H.EFF_END_DTM = '99991231235959'
          AND H.CHRGR_CL_CD = 'Z02E'
          AND H.DEL_YN = '0'
          AND H.PROC_ST_CD  = 'Z0110') Z02E,  -- 원상복구 책임자
      (SELECT F.MR_REQ_NO
             ,listagg(F.DRAW_MNG_NO||':'||F.FILE_NM, '|') WITHIN GROUP(ORDER BY FILE_NM) AS DRAW_MNG_NO_FILE_NM
--            ,listagg(F.DRAW_MNG_NO,'|') WITHIN GROUP(ORDER BY F.DRAW_MNG_NO) AS DRAW_MNG_NO
--            ,listagg(F.FILE_NM,'|') WITHIN GROUP(ORDER BY F.FILE_NM) AS FILE_NM
         FROM MR_ATCH_FILE F
            ,(SELECT *
                FROM MR_REQ_PROC_STEP S
                    ,MR_REQ_PROC_STEP_DET D
               WHERE S.MR_REQ_PROC_STEP_NO = D.MR_REQ_PROC_STEP_NO
                 AND S.MR_STEP_CD IN ('Z0010','Z0020','Z003')
                 AND S.DEL_YN = '0'
                 AND D.DEL_YN = '0'
                 AND D.PROC_ST_CD  = 'Z0110') T1
        WHERE T1.MR_REQ_PROC_STEP_DET_NO = F.MR_REQ_PROC_STEP_DET_NO
          AND F.DRAW_MNG_NO  IS NOT NULL
          AND F.DEL_YN = '0'
        GROUP BY F.MR_REQ_NO) ATTACH,  -- 첨부 파일
      (SELECT S.MR_REQ_NO, S.LAST_CHG_DT
         FROM MR_REQ_PROC_STEP S
        WHERE MR_STEP_CD = 'Z0025'
          AND S.DEL_YN = '0'
          AND S.PROC_ST_CD  = 'Z0131') Z0025,  -- 직무검토(1) 완료일
      (SELECT S.MR_REQ_NO, S.LAST_CHG_DT
         FROM MR_REQ_PROC_STEP S
        WHERE MR_STEP_CD = 'Z0030'
          AND S.DEL_YN = '0'
          AND S.PROC_ST_CD  = 'Z0132') Z0030,  -- 타당성검토 완료일
      (SELECT S.MR_REQ_NO, S.LAST_CHG_DT
         FROM MR_REQ_PROC_STEP S
        WHERE MR_STEP_CD = 'Z0040'
          AND S.DEL_YN = '0'
          AND S.PROC_ST_CD  = 'Z0132') Z0040,  -- 직무검토(2) 완료일
      (SELECT S.MR_REQ_NO, S.LAST_CHG_DT
         FROM MR_REQ_PROC_STEP S
        WHERE MR_STEP_CD = 'Z0050'
          AND S.DEL_YN = '0'
          AND S.PROC_ST_CD  = 'Z0131') Z0050,  -- 투자지품의 완료일
      (SELECT S.MR_REQ_NO, S.LAST_CHG_DT
         FROM MR_REQ_PROC_STEP S
        WHERE MR_STEP_CD = 'Z0060'
          AND S.DEL_YN = '0'
          AND S.PROC_ST_CD  = 'Z0131') Z0060,  -- MR수행 완료일
      (SELECT S.MR_REQ_NO, S.LAST_CHG_DT
         FROM MR_REQ_PROC_STEP S
        WHERE MR_STEP_CD = 'Z0070'
          AND S.DEL_YN = '0'
          AND S.PROC_ST_CD  = 'Z0131') Z0070,  -- 가동전안전점검  완료일
      (SELECT S.MR_REQ_NO, S.LAST_CHG_DT
         FROM MR_REQ_PROC_STEP S
        WHERE MR_STEP_CD = 'Z0080'
          AND S.DEL_YN = '0'
          AND S.PROC_ST_CD  = 'Z0131') Z0080,  -- 자료등록일
      (SELECT S.MR_REQ_NO, S.LAST_CHG_DT
         FROM MR_REQ_PROC_STEP S
        WHERE MR_STEP_CD = 'Z0090'
          AND S.DEL_YN = '0'
          AND S.PROC_ST_CD  = 'Z0131') Z0090,  -- MR완료일
      (SELECT *
         FROM MR_REQ_CHRGR_CHG_HIST H
        WHERE EXISTS (SELECT *
                        FROM MR_REQ_PROC_STEP_DET D
                       WHERE D.MR_STEP_CD = 'Z00R0'
                         AND D.DEL_YN     = '0'
                         AND D.MR_REQ_PROC_STEP_DET_NO = H.MR_REQ_PROC_STEP_DET_NO)
          AND H.EFF_END_DTM = '99991231235959'
          AND H.CHRGR_CL_CD = 'Z02C'
          AND H.DEL_YN      = '0'
          AND H.PROC_ST_CD  = 'Z0110') Z00R0,  -- 위험성검토 승인자
      (SELECT *
         FROM MR_RV_RST R
        WHERE R.ITEM_CD     = 'RISK'
          AND R.DEL_YN      = '0') Z00RC     -- 위험성검토 항목
WHERE M.MR_REQ_NO = Z02A.MR_REQ_NO       -- MR요청자
  AND M.MR_REQ_NO = Z02C1.MR_REQ_NO(+)   -- MR요청 1차 승인자
  AND M.MR_REQ_NO = Z02C2.MR_REQ_NO(+)   -- MR요청 2차 승인자
  AND M.MR_REQ_NO = Z02C3.MR_REQ_NO(+)   -- MR요청 3차 승인자
  AND M.MR_REQ_NO = Z02D.MR_REQ_NO(+)    -- MR 기술검토자
  AND M.MR_REQ_NO = Z02I.MR_REQ_NO(+)    -- MR 기술검토자
  AND M.MR_REQ_NO = Z02G.MR_REQ_NO(+)    -- MR수행 팀장
  AND M.MR_REQ_NO = Z02G1.MR_REQ_NO(+)   -- MR수행직책과장
  AND M.MR_REQ_NO = Z0025.MR_REQ_NO(+)   -- 직무검토(1) 완료일
  AND M.MR_REQ_NO = Z0030.MR_REQ_NO(+)   -- 타당성검토 완료일
  AND M.MR_REQ_NO = Z0040.MR_REQ_NO(+)   -- 직무검토(2) 완료일
  AND M.MR_REQ_NO = Z0050.MR_REQ_NO(+)   -- 투자지품의 완료일
  AND M.MR_REQ_NO = Z0060.MR_REQ_NO(+)   -- MR수행 완료일
  AND M.MR_REQ_NO = Z0070.MR_REQ_NO(+)   -- 가동전안전점검일
  AND M.MR_REQ_NO = Z0080.MR_REQ_NO(+)   -- 자료등록일
  AND M.MR_REQ_NO = Z0090.MR_REQ_NO(+)   -- MR완료일
  AND M.MR_REQ_NO = Z00R0.MR_REQ_NO(+)   -- 위험성검토 승인자
  AND M.MR_REQ_NO = Z00RC.MR_REQ_NO(+)   -- 위험성검토 항목
  AND M.MR_REQ_NO = UNIT.MR_REQ_NO(+)    -- 세부공정
  AND M.PLANT     = UNIT.WERKS(+)        -- 세부공정
  AND M.MR_REQ_NO = EQUIP.MR_REQ_NO(+)   -- 관련설비
  AND M.MR_REQ_NO = Z02E.MR_REQ_NO(+)    -- 원상복구 책임자
  AND M.MR_REQ_NO = ATTACH.MR_REQ_NO(+)  -- 첨부 파일
  AND M.MR_NO LIKE '20%'
  AND M.PROC_ST_CD <> 'Z0143'
  AND M.DEL_YN    = '0'
--  AND M.MR_REQ_NO = 4760
ORDER BY 1 DESC
;
--------------------------------------------------------
--  DDL for View V_MR_PROC_STEP
--------------------------------------------------------

  CREATE OR REPLACE FORCE EDITIONABLE VIEW "HDOEDIMS"."V_MR_PROC_STEP" ("MR_REQ_PROC_STEP_NO", "MR_REQ_NO", "MR_STEP_CD", "PROC_ST_CD", "EFF_END_DTM", "EFF_STA_DTM", "DEL_YN", "FST_RGST_DT", "FST_RGSTR", "LAST_CHG_DT", "LAST_CHGR") AS SELECT 
    MR_REQ_PROC_STEP_NO,
    MR_REQ_NO,
    MR_STEP_CD,
    PROC_ST_CD,
    EFF_END_DTM,
    EFF_STA_DTM,
    DEL_YN,
    FST_RGST_DT,
    FST_RGSTR,
    LAST_CHG_DT,
    LAST_CHGR
FROM (
    SELECT 
        PS.*,
        CASE 
            WHEN PS.MR_STEP_CD = 'Z0040' AND PS.PROC_ST_CD IN ('Z0110', 'Z0131', 'Z0132') THEN
                COUNT(*) OVER(PARTITION BY MR_REQ_NO, MR_STEP_CD) 
            ELSE 1
        END AS TOTAL_COUNT,
        CASE 
            WHEN PS.MR_STEP_CD = 'Z0040' AND PS.PROC_ST_CD IN ('Z0110', 'Z0131', 'Z0132') THEN
                ROW_NUMBER() OVER(PARTITION BY MR_REQ_NO, MR_STEP_CD ORDER BY FST_RGST_DT DESC, PROC_ST_CD DESC)
            ELSE 1
        END AS RN
    FROM 
        MR_REQ_PROC_STEP PS
    WHERE 
        PS.DEL_YN = 0
)
WHERE 
    MR_STEP_CD != 'Z0040'
    OR 
    (
        MR_STEP_CD = 'Z0040' AND 
        (
            NOT(PROC_ST_CD IN ('Z0110', 'Z0131', 'Z0132'))
            OR
            (PROC_ST_CD IN ('Z0110', 'Z0131', 'Z0132') AND (TOTAL_COUNT = 1 OR (TOTAL_COUNT >= 2 AND RN = 1)))
        )
    )
;
--------------------------------------------------------
--  DDL for View V_MR_TASK_DATA
--------------------------------------------------------

  CREATE OR REPLACE FORCE EDITIONABLE VIEW "HDOEDIMS"."V_MR_TASK_DATA" ("MR_REQ_NO", "MR_NO", "CHRG_EMP_NO", "CL_CHG_DT", "CHRGR_CL_CD", "CL_CD_01", "CL01_TEXT", "CL_CD_02", "CL02_TEXT", "CL_CD_03", "CL03_TEXT", "CL_CD_05", "CL05_TEXT", "CL_TEXT", "TOT_RV_SUGG", "DRAW_MNG_NO_FILE_NM", "MR_STEP_CD", "PROC_ST_CD", "FST_RGST_DT", "LAST_CHG_DT") AS SELECT H.MR_REQ_NO
            , M.MR_NO
            , H.CHRG_EMP_NO
            , TO_CHAR(R.LAST_CHG_DT,'YYYY-MM-DD') CL_CHG_DT
            , H.CHRGR_CL_CD
            , R.CL_CD_01
            , CASE
                WHEN R.CL_CMT_01 IS NOT NULL THEN R.CL_CMT_01
                ELSE ' '
              END AS CL01_TEXT
            , R.CL_CD_02
            , CASE
                WHEN R.CL_CMT_01 IS NOT NULL THEN R.CL_CMT_02
                ELSE ' '
              END AS CL02_TEXT
            , R.CL_CD_03
            , CASE
                WHEN R.CL_CMT_01 IS NOT NULL THEN R.CL_CMT_03
                ELSE ' '
              END AS CL03_TEXT
            , R.CL_CD_05
            , CASE
                WHEN R.CL_CMT_01 IS NOT NULL THEN R.CL_CMT_05
                ELSE ' '
              END AS CL05_TEXT

            , CASE
                WHEN R.CL_CD_02 IS NULL THEN R.CL_CMT_02
                WHEN R.CL_CD_03 IS NULL THEN R.CL_CMT_03
                WHEN R.CL_CD_05 IS NULL THEN R.CL_CMT_05
                WHEN R.CL_CD_06 IS NULL THEN R.CL_CMT_06
                ELSE ''
              END AS CL_TEXT
            , R.TOT_RV_SUGG
            , CASE
                WHEN F5.FILE_STEP_CD = '0502' THEN F5.DRAW_MNG_NO_FILE_NM
                ELSE ' '
              END AS DRAW_MNG_NO_FILE_NM
            , M.MR_STEP_CD
            , M.PROC_ST_CD
            , M.FST_RGST_DT
            , M.LAST_CHG_DT
         FROM MR_REQ_MST M
             ,MR_REQ_CHRGR_CHG_HIST H
             ,MR_RV_RST R
            ,(SELECT F.MR_REQ_NO, F.MR_REQ_PROC_STEP_DET_NO, FILE_STEP_CD, FILE_CD
                    ,listagg(F.DRAW_MNG_NO||':'||F.FILE_NM, '|') WITHIN GROUP(ORDER BY FILE_NM) AS DRAW_MNG_NO_FILE_NM
                    --,listagg(F.DRAW_MNG_NO,',') WITHIN GROUP(ORDER BY F.DRAW_MNG_NO) AS DRAW_MNG_NO
                    --,listagg(F.FILE_NM,',') WITHIN GROUP(ORDER BY F.FILE_NM) AS FILE_NM
                FROM MR_ATCH_FILE F
               WHERE F.DRAW_MNG_NO  IS NOT NULL
                 AND F.FILE_STEP_CD = '0502'
                 AND F.DEL_YN = '0'
               GROUP BY F.MR_REQ_NO, F.MR_REQ_PROC_STEP_DET_NO, FILE_STEP_CD, FILE_CD) F5  -- 첨부 파일
        WHERE EXISTS (SELECT *
                        FROM MR_REQ_PROC_STEP S
                            ,MR_REQ_PROC_STEP_DET D
                       WHERE S.MR_REQ_PROC_STEP_NO = D.MR_REQ_PROC_STEP_NO
                         AND S.MR_STEP_CD = 'Z0040'
                         AND S.DEL_YN     = '0'
                         AND D.DEL_YN     = '0'
                         AND D.PROC_ST_CD  = 'Z0110'
                         AND D.MR_REQ_PROC_STEP_DET_NO = H.MR_REQ_PROC_STEP_DET_NO)
          --AND H.MR_REQ_NO = 4397
          AND M.MR_REQ_NO = H.MR_REQ_NO
          AND M.MR_REQ_NO = F5.MR_REQ_NO(+)
          AND H.EFF_END_DTM = '99991231235959'
          AND H.CHRGR_CL_CD in ('Z02H9','Z02H10','Z02H11')
          AND H.DEL_YN      = '0'
          AND H.PROC_ST_CD  = 'Z0110'
          AND R.CL_CD_01  IS NOT NULL
          AND H.MR_REQ_PROC_STEP_DET_NO = R.MR_REQ_PROC_STEP_DET_NO
          AND H.MR_REQ_PROC_STEP_DET_NO = F5.MR_REQ_PROC_STEP_DET_NO(+)
          AND M.PROC_ST_CD <> 'Z0143'
          AND M.DEL_YN = '0'
          ORDER BY 1
;
